if (!is_file('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/autoload_static.php');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/autoload_static.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php') != '405ab39e189537fc1a5f5afef0bf4e6820729702') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/autoload_static.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/autoload_static.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php') !== '405ab39e189537fc1a5f5afef0bf4e6820729702') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php') !== '2c122d37f4618faafd39f7038677bf50f769fadc') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/autoload_static.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php') !== '405ab39e189537fc1a5f5afef0bf4e6820729702') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/autoload_static.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_18();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != '946b514dc923a6d6e6e45c7d38503598b393fead') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '946b514dc923a6d6e6e45c7d38503598b393fead') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '20e8414211ae395b4d2816257a10749573d85523') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_18();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '946b514dc923a6d6e6e45c7d38503598b393fead') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.php');
	writefile_19();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') != 'cdb7ac05818dfe0251069f72568cba2c39e0aab3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== 'cdb7ac05818dfe0251069f72568cba2c39e0aab3') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '18800a111edcb221d653dec7464b8c5936c03a08') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_19();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== 'cdb7ac05818dfe0251069f72568cba2c39e0aab3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
		}
	}
}
